fàantan fìla lá tériya, ù sí tɛ́ nàta  sí nɔ̀ fɛ̀kúran bɛ́ kɛ́ kà ízini látaama...kúran bɛ́ kɛ́ kà ízini látaama...kàrisa ɲɛ́ nátaliye táa'ń bɛ́í k'í bólo láteliya  báara lá !í k'í bólo láteliya  báara lá !ní  bì sú ìn nátɛmɛnaà bɛ́ kúma  kà kúma  kà jùru látɛmɛ :bálimasira wɛ́rɛ tɛ́  mín bɛ́  àle látɛmɛí yɛ̀rɛ látɛmɛ  Ála màní  bì sú ìn nátɛmɛnaà bɛ́ kúma  kà kúma  kà jùru látɛmɛ :bálimasira wɛ́rɛ tɛ́  mín bɛ́  àle látɛmɛí yɛ̀rɛ látɛmɛ  Ála màà yé  né látigɛ  kúrun náí y'í ká mùru látigɛ wá ?án kɔ̀ni tɛ́ sé k'à látigɛ, án kà  à yɛ̀rɛ wéle kà nàà hákili látigɛlen dònmɔ̀gɔ bɛ́  láyidu tà, Ála b'ó látiimɛmɔ̀gɔ bɛ́  láyidu tà, Ála b'ó látiimɛkàrisa ní rɔ́tiyɛnnaí yé  kàrisa látiyɛn  né màkàrisa ní rɔ́tiyɛnnaí yé  kàrisa látiyɛn  né màkɔ̀nɔnin kélen tɛ́ sé  kà dénmisɛnnin fìla látulonjí látɔnò tú látɔnnenkɔ̀nɔnin kélen tɛ́ sé  kà dénmisɛnnin fìla látulonkàtugu  tílennenya yé  sí látunubali yékàtugu  tílennenya yé  sí látunubali yéné yé à láwasa àlikama ní ɛ̀rɛzɛndɔlɔ lá (gn 27, 37)à y'á láwuli  ò kámakà ù láwoyo kɔ̀ kɔ́nɔà y'á láwuli  ò kámaàrajo kán láyɛlɛnà bɛ́ kà à ká kàbasen yéelen láyelenku cógo mín ná, é bɛ́ ò dɔ́n wá?báara láyiriwa /

kɔ̀lɔnda nɔ́rɔkɔlen  mɔ̀gɔ fɛ̀nìn npàra júguyara dɛ́à yé ù npɛ̀rɛ bɔ́npɛ́ri bɔ́npáyi t'á láà y’à npère` wàaà yé ù npɛ̀rɛ bɔ́bèrekete yɛ̀lɛmabèrekete yɛ̀lɛmaà ye npèreketenin` dí ń màjɛ́gɛ npereketeninnpɛ́ri bɔ́à cámanba bɛ́ npíya !à cámanba bɛ́ npíya !npo cì
à bòlila  kà bɔ́ kàso lá  kà npó cì fɔ́ Dákarià y'á npògotigiya tàjùru npòlokira ń bóloà yé  kàlan npólonà npólonnanpɔ̀lɔn gɔ̀sinpòn bìla kàrisa lápòro tìgɛháli npɔ́rɔ t'á láà yé ù npɛ̀rɛ bɔ́jɛ́gɛ yé  bùre cìà bɛ́ nsàna dásánpɔ̀rɔn bɔ́ / cì à ládénmisɛnnin sɔ́mi má sé  báara mín kɛ́li yé, ń'í kó : à k'ò kɛ́, í b'á bànansíirin dánsíirin dásíra mìn
síra fòronnsìranɛgɛ nùgulensɔ́lɔ yé fàn ni ɲɔ́gɔn cɛ́ yédénmisɛnnin sɔ́mi má sé  báara mín kɛ́li yé, ń'í kó : à k'ò kɛ́, í b'á bànansón dára  mùru ìn náá' yé  nsòn bɛ̀n !né má  mɔ̀gɔ sí sònya ábadantàlen dántàlen dákúma kɔ́rɔntan`à bɛ́ ntàntantan ná mɔ̀gɔ dáfɛ̀/nɔ̀fɛ̀- ntɛ́ɛntɛ- mísakà ntɛ́gɛnw dílan, kà ntɛ́gɛnw sìgincɔ̀gɔn b'á láà ye tɛ́lɛ dá à ɲɛ́
à ye ntɛ́lɛ cì/sàra/dòn à lá- ntɛ́ɛntɛ- mísadénmisɛn y'á téntegema sìgilan kànntìiri cìà tìrintira kà bìn dùgu màwùlu bɛ ù nún tìrinti-tìrinti dùgu mà à kása bólosúgujɔ kɛ́ra ń-tìn-kà-dɔ́n yé à bólo
né ká kɛ́len bɛ́ɛ tìn-kà-dɔ́n bɛ́ ń nántìiri cìntúlo kélen bɛ́ tìgɛ kà bɔ́ ntúloma náfɛ́n dɔ́ bálanna  à ngɔ̀ki láà táara í sìgi ò ntòn kùncɛ rɔ́dònso bɛ́  jí tà  k'à bɔ̀n ntòn ná wáasa kà sògo sɔ̀rɔí kàna án ntɔ́gɔntɔgɔ cì án kɔ́nɔ !síniwa bɛ́na ntòlatankɛnɛ 3 jɔ̀ Màli lántòmo nàkun yé  dɔ̀n yéà táara í sìgi ò ntòn kùncɛ rɔ́dònso bɛ́  jí tà  k'à bɔ̀n ntòn ná wáasa kà sògo sɔ̀rɔfárakuru bón k'à ntóni, ò tɛ́  bólo-dá-ń-dá-lá bɔ́à bɛ ntòntonton` ná mɔ̀gɔw kɔ́ba fara fɔ kà ntòolonìn dénnin ntɔ́rɔn ká bòn kójugukàmiden tɔ́rɔla bìtìga fàrama bɛ́ tɔ́rɔ kà wɔ́rɔà y'á tà  kà tɔ́rɔ  dùgu màkà tùfa gòsiù bɛ́  ntùgun wúliù bɛ́  ntùgun wúlintúlo kélen bɛ́ tìgɛ kà bɔ́ ntúloma nání  sìlantumu má jìgin, myɛ̀tɔ nà yɛ̀lɛnsúgujɔ kɛ́ra ń-tìn-kà-dɔ́n yé à bólo

sà bɛ́ kálanso  jíri bólo lákálata bɛ́na kɛ́ jámana tílali lá (nb 26, 55)sán 2007 kàlata bɛ́ lábɛn  sáriya kúra tàlen nìnnu húkumu kɔ́nɔà y'í kàli  bási lá...àn k'án kàli  dɔ́rɔmɛ fìla láà y'í kàli  bási lá...àn k'án kàli  dɔ́rɔmɛ fìla láń kàlifa b'í láà yé  mìsi kélen kàlifa  à màà y'í kàli  bási lá...àn k'án kàli  dɔ́rɔmɛ fìla láń kàlifa b'í láà yé  mìsi kélen kàlifa  à màà y'í kàli  bási lá...àn k'án kàli  dɔ́rɔmɛ fìla láà dònna káluwa lákáliya bɔ́takálo dònna  sú rɔ́kálo kúra
kálo sàlen
kà kálo sàba jàlen kɛ́à yé  kálo bìlaà dònna káluwa láÁla kámàà wúlila né kámàɲɛ́ŋunu dàn yé  kàmakun yéà ká kámalenmàa tɛ́ sé kà  à ká kámalenya kɛ́  ń'á má  fìliko kélen kɛ́màa dùsu kàmalifɛ́n kàmamamàa dùsu kàmalià táara  kàmakɔrɔsɔgɔsira fɛ̀màa dùsu kàmalitásuma kàminakán tìgɛ
dùlɔkijɛ bɛ́  à kán ná
jùru bɛ́  à kán ná
à yé  màrifa dá  à kán ná
fàlaka bɛ́  à kán ná
fìni bɔ́  í kán nákánnabɔnɔ́ɔrɔ bɛ́  à kán ná
à kán ká dí
à kán sìsilen dòn
í kán kɔ́rɔta !
í kán bɛ́  né mà wá ?
à kán bɛ́ ní é yé
í kán dòn
ń'í má  màa kán mɛ́, í ná tó  í kélen ná
kán t'á lá
kán bìla
à y'á kán mìnɛ ( lámɛn )à bɛ́ sé  kán cáman nákárikan
jiwoyokanù ka kánò ni kɛ́ ka kán
à ka kán ní...yé
ò tùn man kán  kà kɛ́
nê ka kán  kà mùn kɛ́ ?
à man kán tɛ́ kà...bíyɛn kán màa náyɛ̀lɛn  sò kàn
k'à dá  mùn kàn ?
kɛ́nɛ kàn
í kùn dá  Ntègedo kàn
yé  dɔ́gɔ dá  k'à bìla  síbiri kàn
à nàta bɛ́  wári kànán bɛ́na kúma  ŋúnu dílacogo dè kàn :fɔ́lifɔla bɛ́  fɔ́li kàn k'à fɔ́ :fɛ́n dá  fɛ́n kàn / fɛ́n fàra  fɛ́n kàn / fɛ́n bìla  fɛ́n kàn :
tán d'á mà, kàna tɛ̀mɛ  ò kàn !à táara dòn  Ncì kànÁla kà  án kùlu fá,  à kàna  án bá fá !
í kàna kàsi !à bɛ́ síran  à kàna sàí kánbila màa màù kán dí  ɲɔ́gɔn mà kónê ma kànkari dá í yé wà ?bá yé  kàngarimada  à dénmuso yé kó : sú kàna kò  k'à tó  bɔ́lɔn nán'í ye í dén wéle kó: "fàama", à bɛ nísɔngɔ káni mɔ̀gɔ fɔ́lɔ mîn ná, ò yé ê yésyɛ̀ mána  kíli dá, à bɛ́ kánkanɲɛ́nɛ kànkàn dá lá !à kánkanna bɔ́ranê ma kànkari dá í yé wà ?bá yé  kàngarimada  à dénmuso yé kó : sú kàna kò  k'à tó  bɔ́lɔn náné kánkɔnɔna bɛ́ ń dímiÁla kámàà wúlila né kámàí kánmàdá à fà ń'á bá yénɛ̀gɛ kánɲɛfà yé  à dénmuso kánnabila  ò cɛ̀ yé :kánnabɔ yé  màa kúra yé  mín bɛ́  kɔ̀rɔlen  sènkɔrɔí yé  sù mín kánnajuru sàra...í kà ń kánnaminɛ ò kɔ́ !nɛ̀gɛ kánɲɛkánntanyakobólo kálanso  ɲɔ́gɔn ná

bólo kálanso  màa kán ná
sà bɛ́ kálanso  jíri bólo lásyɛ̀ bɛ́ kántigɛ ní fúruyiidikuma yéà yé  dúmuni kɛ́  fɔ́ à kántigɛdasyɛ̀kan yé  kántigɛla tá yémín máa kɛ́ k'á kántigɛ, á' yé  kántigɛla d'ó màkántigiya mán ɲì  fàn kélen fɛ̀í yé  mín fɔ́, í y'á bɔ́  ò síra fɛ̀, í kántigiyaraù y'á kànu...ù y'á kànu...kànuɲɔgɔnman cɛ́kɛlɛkànuɲɔgɔnman cɛ́kɛlɛà bá kànuya b'á lá kósɛbɛù y'á kànuya...í kɛ́nyɛna ní  à túma yé
kà dòni kɛ́nyɛ  fàli kɔ́ rɔ́
à yé sàya kɛ́nyɛ ń'á yé
í kàna  mɔ̀gɔjugu ní  mɔ̀gɔ tílennen kɛ́nyɛÁla kà  án kùlu fá,  à kàna  án bá fá !
í kàna kàsi !à bɛ́ síran  à kàna sàfàama kɛ̀lɛbaa, kára b'á lákà kára` bìn à kànà kàlan ká dímàa tɛ́ kɔ̀rɔ  kàlan mà
kàlan kùn fɔ́lɔ
kàlan kùn fílananà bɛ́ kàlan kɛ́  dénmisɛn kùnkàra bɔ́tùma sébali tɛ́ kárabakàrama dá  màa kànò mísali ìn bɔ́ra kàramɔgɔdegesɛbɛn kɔ́nɔ...káran kɛ́ra kó fìla mà : kàlan àni kɛ́nɛyakoà kàrangafe bɔ́lenkárisu
kári ntɛ̀nɛntankárimuru
à kɔ́nɔ kárilen dòn
jìgi kárià táara  fúra kárinɛ́nɛ kárila à láà y'í kári  só kɔ́nɔí nà dòn kàro lá bìnìn wùlu ka kásanà bɛ́ bɛ́ɛ kàsaara sònyaliko láí kàsabakɔrɔ sɔ̀nna  nìn mà ! :wári kàsabi yé  jòli yé ?à y'í bàn kásakià ɲí bɛ́ kɛ́nɛ kàn kásakinìn wùlu ka kásanà bɛ́ bɛ́ɛ kàsaara sònyaliko láí kásaya  màa fɛ̀dòno kàsirané má (kó) fóyi kɛ́ mín ká kán ní kàsoladonni yé (gn 40, 15)bólo kálanso  ɲɔ́gɔn ná

ù tùn bɛ́  kà yɛ́lɛ bɔ́  à mà  kɛ̀rɛ fɛ̀ń bɛ́ ń bólo kɛ́rɛnkɛrɛn  nìn wári kànkɛ̀rɛnkɛrɛn fɛ̀kɛ́rɛnkɛrɛnnenya láÀlé sèginbagatɔ́`, à ká bàbí` kérewera.mángoro kèrun ní  bére yésúgunɛkɛ bɛ́  fìni ngèsenbàna yé  dénmisɛn ìn ngèsenà yé  kó kɛ́ta kɛ́dén b'í ɲɛ́mada  à bá ká kɛ́ta fɛ̀ (mà)màa sògo tɛ́ dún, í kɛ́wale dè bɛ́ dúnwɔ̀lɔ ká kègun ní sònsan yéà y'á kìbaroya mɛ́ kúnuà y'á kìbaroya mɛ́ kúnukíri tɛ́ dùgakɔrɔ ní wùlusu cɛ́
kíri tìgɛ màa kàn
kíri bìn màa kànù yé sòn cì fɔ́ k'á kìrikarafúra ká sùrun kà kɛ́  tìɲɛ yé  kà tɛ̀mɛ  kílisi kànù yé sòn cì fɔ́ k'á kìrikarakíri tɛ́ dùgakɔrɔ ní wùlusu cɛ́
kíri tìgɛ màa kàn
kíri bìn màa kànkíli dá
kíli tɔ́rɔkɔ̀mɔkiliá' yé  kàrisa kíli  kà nà yànfúra ká sùrun kà kɛ́  tìɲɛ yé  kà tɛ̀mɛ  kílisi kàni bè koliriji (i n'a fò « kiloranfenikòliji ») tòni ko fila kè a nyèw kan, sògòma ani su, bana waati bèe kònò.Fàlajɛ kìn yé  sàba yékínibolo tɛ́ màga  à lá, númabolo kɔ́yɔ́rɔ cáman bón dá dè bɛ́ yɛ̀lɛ  í kínifɛla fɛ̀kínibolo tɛ́ màga  à lá, númabolo kɔ́yɔ́rɔ cáman bón dá dè bɛ́ yɛ̀lɛ  í kínifɛla fɛ̀Ála káma, kíra kámakíri tɛ́ dùgakɔrɔ ní wùlusu cɛ́
kíri tìgɛ màa kàn
kíri bìn màa kàndíkolen y'á kìribií kàna ń ká fìni kòlen kùrubukaraba dɛ́ !ù yé sòn cì fɔ́ k'á kìrikarasán fìnna kírikirisán fìnna kírikirià kìrinnanɛ́nɛ y'á sèn kìrinfúra ká sùrun kà kɛ́  tìɲɛ yé  kà tɛ̀mɛ  kílisi kànsán fìnna kírikirií bɛ́  kìsɛ bɔ́  mángorokolo lá

Ála m'án kísira  ò mà !í ká kán  kà màa kísi ní  ɲùman yéù yé sòn cì fɔ́ k'á kìrikarakíri tɛ́ dùgakɔrɔ ní wùlusu cɛ́

màa kɔ́ dòn  ɲɔ́gɔn màà y'í kɔ́ fílɛsánji` bɛ tìgɛ k'à kɔ́` tó ngómi` yékálo kélen ní kɔ́kɔ́bɔà y'á kɔ́  kàlifa  né màà yé  dùlɔki dòn  à kɔ́ kàn
à y'á fɔ́  à kɔ́ kànfílen kɔ́ tìgɛ ní  fù yéà y'á fɔ́  à kɔ́ kánò kɛŕa nê kɔ́
à tɛ táa mîn kɔ́, à tɛ́ ɲà mîn kɔ́sɛ̀nɛfɛn sí má ɲà, màlo kɔ́kɔ̀ bɛ́ dònkɔ̀ díyaramùso kòbikɔ́bi kɛ́mùso kòbikɔ́bi kɛ́à yé  kɔ́di ń màÁla k'à kɔ́falen  sìma ná !à kɔ́fasa kànɲɔ́gɔn kɔ́fɛ̀dén dɔ́ bɛ́ nà  ù kɔ́fɛla kànń y'á sàn kɛ̀mɛ  k'à kɔ́filiń yé  fɛ́n mín kó'í yé, í m'ó dí ń máà ye kógo tà kà dòn à ka sóà kɔ́gɔ fálen
kɔ́gɔ dá à lá
kɔ́gɔ dá  fìni ná, fɛ́n cɛ̀  kɔ́gɔ lá, fɛ́n súma  kɔ́gɔ láà dénmuso má kɔ́gɔ bánkɔ̀gɔ bɔ́len  à lá
kɔ̀gɔ kɔ́rɔdoní bólo kɔ̀gɔ bɔ́dényɛrɛnin sàta nìnnu ná, 20% ká sàya sábabu yé ù kɔ́gɔbaliya yéà bɛ́  dɔ̀lɔ mìn kójugukójùgu ! ń dára  ò láà kúlo kójuguya y'á kán sìsià ye kógo tà kà dòn à ka sókɔ̀gɔ bɔ́len  à lá

bólo kálanso  màa kán ná

à kɔ̀lila móbilisɔngɔ láwɔ̀lɔkɔrɔ dòn, kɔ̀yi sàba b'á lákòlila bɛ́ sɔ̀rɔà bòonsi kúlelen bìlen ní jɛ́à yɛ̀rɛ̂ kólo lá

kùn kɔ́miFàma ka fìsa kominike ye.kɔ́rɔtigɛlikan tɛ́  jèli dòn  kɔ̀mɔ ná kó : syɛ̀sogo ká díkón sɔ̀gɔkɔ́n fyɛ́ = fìle fyɛ́sáni kà  bɔ́nbɔn fìli, dénmisɛnnin bɛ́ɛ kɔ́nnen dòndɔ́ bɛ́ kɔ̀n ń ɲɛ́
án nà kɔ̀n  kà dúmuni kɛ́ bìné ká kóɲɛ má ɲà fɔ́lɔní  mùso kóɲɛ fɔ́lɔ dòn, à bɛ́ fɔ́ kó : Ncì, ní  sènɲa fílanan dòn, à bɛ́ fɔ́ kó : Nsànwólo tɛ́  kònaya sàyáala y'á kònayané ká kóɲɛ má ɲà fɔ́lɔní  mùso kóɲɛ fɔ́lɔ dòn, à bɛ́ fɔ́ kó : Ncì, ní  sènɲa fílanan dòn, à bɛ́ fɔ́ kó : Nsànní kɔ́ɲɔ bɛ́ bɔ́, jí bɛ́ sìgi  kɔ́ɲɔmuso kùn, mìnni kámakɔ́ngɔba bìrasùmɛ dánin gɔ̀ngɔlilenà yé  né lámara, ò má  háli gɔ̀ngɔli sìgi né kùnnìn kɔ̀ni tɛ́ sàlabaatɔ yéà bòonsi kúlelen bìlen ní jɛ́né ká jìginɛ kónkonnadá kɔ́nkɔnà yé dá gɔ̀si  "kɔ́n-kɔ́n-kɔ́n'à yé dén tà  à kɔ̀nkɔn náà yé dá gɔ̀si  "kɔ́n-kɔ́n-kɔ́n'á b'á dá  á kɔ́nɔ kàn

jírifɛɛrɛn kɔ́nɔ ká bònkɔ́nɔ tón  jùru láfèerelikɛla yé ń kɔ́nɔní kɔ́ɲɔ bɛ́ bɔ́, jí bɛ́ sìgi  kɔ́ɲɔmuso kùn, mìnni kámasyɔ̀ yé  kɔ̀nɔ tìgɛmùso kɔ́nɔbaratigikɔ́nɔbara fàsa b'án tànga kɔ́nɔbaya màù y'á kɔ́ɲɔbɔ  wáa mùgankɔ́nɔcibange bɛ́ kɛ́ fú lá Màli fàn tán ní náani lámìnnifilen kɔ́nɔba àni kɔ́nɔduná kàna á jìgi dá kɔ́nɔfɔɲɔgɔn kànɲínɛ kɔ́nɔma bɛ́, jàkuma kɔ́nɔma bɛ́, dɔ́ dén bɛ́ kɛ́  kà dɔ́ báloɲɔ̀tɛli yé kɔ́nɔmaya dáminɛkàbi  à kɔ́nɔmayara, à ní  bàna dònàle dè bɛ́ né bɔ́ kɔ̀nɔminɛla ká ján náàle dè bɛ́ né bɔ́ kɔ̀nɔminɛla ká ján nákɔ́nɔ tón  jùru láfèerelikɛla yé ń kɔ́nɔdén bɛ́ lámaga  à bá kɔ́nɔna dè lá :bángen kɔ́nɔna nɔ́í kà í kɔ́nɔnakuru cì ù kàn í ká Dími wáati lá! /  Né nà né kɔ́nɔnakuru bɛ́ɛ cì i kànà táara bɔ́ ń yé  k'í kɔ́nɔnandiya  né kɔ́rɔ kósɛbɛbî kɔ̀nɔntɔnbî kɔ̀nɔntɔnsí má  sí ɲìninka  í kɔ́nɔta láKo dɔnkilidakan bɛ, ne m'o kɔnpran kosɛbɛ, nka n tulo bɛ dɔnkilidakan na.(Thoyer, Contes, Fane 1997)à yé  né mìnɛ kóɲumandɔ́gɔ y'í ɲɛ́don  à kɔ̀rɔ lákɔ̀rɔ ká júgu dɛ́ !kálo kòolilen bɛ́kɔ́nɔmaya láɲinibali kɔ̀lɔlɔ yé jùmɛn yé ?kálo kòolilen bɛ́jí kɛ́ kóro lákɔ́sa tɛ fɔ́ bínɲimina mà fùru kɔ́kà kɔ́rɔɲɔn` sìgi, kà kɔ́rɔɲɔn` jɔ̀kàrisa kórilen bɛ́  só kɔ́nɔkɔ̀r'í ká kɛ́nɛ ?jí kɛ́ kóro láń má kóro fɔ́lɔwɔ̀lɔkɔrɔ

bàkɔrɔnkɔ́rɔn fɛ̀kà kɔ́rɔɲɔn` sìgi, kà kɔ́rɔɲɔn` jɔ̀kà kɔ́rɔɲɔn` sìgi, kà kɔ́rɔɲɔn` jɔ̀à y'á kùn kɔ́rɔtaní  kɔ́rɔtɔ dòn...kɔ́rɔtɔ mán ɲì, nàfa t'ó lá, nímisa kɔ́ :à kɔ́rɔtɔra  fúru kɔ́rɔ
sù kɔ́rɔtɔra cógo ó cógo, à nà  à tàbaa kɔ̀nɔbàna y'á kɔ̀rɔyakɔ̀r'í ká kɛ́nɛ ?kɔ́sa tɛ fɔ́ bínɲimina mà fùru kɔ́kɔ́sa tɛ fɔ́ bínɲimina mà fùru kɔ́kɔ́sa ìn náà ká màasɛbɛya kɔ́sarakɔ́sa ìn náí kàsabakɔrɔ sɔ̀nna  nìn mà ! :kɔ́sa ìn nákɔ́sa ìn náò kósɔn...ù kɔ́sɔnnenba dònò kósɔn...í yé  Ála kòtaÁlako kàlanbaa ká kòta fànga ká bònní ù kɛ́ra dègun kɔ́tigɛbali yé, mùso ká kán kà sé fúrakɛso láà kɔ̀rɔla kɔ́tɔkɔtɔà kɔ̀rɔla kɔ́tɔkɔtɔkótoɲɔgɔntala bɛ́ kàratabugu sì cáya :kótoɲɔgɔntala bɛ́ kàratabugu sì cáya :à yé  góya kɛ́  né ládùgukolo góyaramá  fóyi góya  í dén náí bɛ́ fàga kɔ́yi !ń má dá  à lá kɔ́yi !í bɛ́ fàga kɔ́yi !ń má dá  à lá kɔ́yi !sàlaya bɛ́ mɔ̀gɔ kɔ̀li
à kɔ̀lila móbilisɔngɔ láwɔ̀lɔkɔrɔ dòn, kɔ̀yi sàba b'á lákɔ́nɔmaya láɲinibali kɔ̀lɔlɔ yé jùmɛn yé ?kà kú bɔ́kú tàí kú tà kà bɔ́ yèn !tìga ní  wóso má kú  ɲìnan :ɲɔ̀ má kún jìginɛ kɔ́nɔí tɛ́ kún à lá bìlenà bɛ́ dími kúnbàna má kún à lákɔ́ngɔ tùma, mɔ̀gɔ tùn bɛ́  kúbɔà bòonsi kúlelen bìlen ní jɛ́á ɲɛ́nasisilenba yé kúlokanba bɔ́ (gn 27, 34)à bòonsi kúlelen bìlen ní jɛ́bólo kálanso  ɲɔ́gɔn ná

bɛ́ɛ ń'í tá kùnda : bámana, fúla...à b'á kùndá Búmudo kànà táara à kùndogo bàtoso gàsimaba dɔ́ kɔ́nɔmàa kùnpa bɔ́né kùnpalen tóra tènmàa kùnpa bɔ́né kùnpalen tóra tèndíɲɛ kó yé  kùnfɛtɔ kó yé : à bé bɛ̀n wó, à tɛ́ bɛ̀n wó, í tɛ́  ò dɔ́nsùmankura kùnfɔlɔ / sɛ̀nɛmɔ kùnfɔlɔ /fúnankɛya kùnfɔlɔkà kúngo díya í lá !kúngo b'á láà bɛ́  kúngokolon táama
à táara  kúngokolon fàntan bántanà bɛ́  kúngokolon táama

tɛ́rɛnkunkoloń yé  kúma kùnkɔ́ri kúnu'Né bɛ́na sàn wólonwula báara kɛ́ í yé, í dénmuso dɔ́gɔmannin Àrasɛli kùnkɔ́rɔ
"Í bɛ́na fɛ́n jùmɛn bìla  kùnkɔ́rɔ ?' / Í ká ɛ̀rɛzɛnforo dí né mà wári kùnkɔ́rɔkúma kùnkurun dɔ́ bɛ́ ń fɛ̀ kà f'í yé
ń yé  tìle bɛ́ɛ kɛ́  sùnɔgɔ lá  ká sú kùnkurun kɛ́...à kùnma ká dɔ́gɔà kùnma ká dɔ́gɔdénmisɛn tɔ̀nɔmadalen kùnmabɔraà y'à fà kùnmabɔ́ kàbánwáraba kùnmafalen yé  dén yéKùnmasicɛ yé né dègun.à kùnna ká kɛ́nɛ
í kùnna ká díà bɛ́ fógon  jí kùnnádùnu ìn bɛ́ fɔ́  hɛ́rɛ kùnnáà sìgitɔ fílɛ  dùgu kùnnájí yé bárasi kùnnadáń'í y'á mɛ́ kó : jɔ̀nnin kùnnandi, à fɔ́ "sábabu ɲúman"ní  fàrigan mɛ́na  dén ná k'à sɔ̀rɔ  kùnnafoni jɔ́njɔn má sɔ̀rɔ  à lá...dén bàra kùnnana bɛ́ fìn  k'à sɔ̀rɔ  jóli bɛ́  à jùkɔrɔla láà yé  sánujala dɔ́ dòn  à kùn ná  kùnnamini sán fɛ̀à kùnna ká kɛ́nɛ
í kùnna ká dídén bàra kùnnana bɛ́ fìn  k'à sɔ̀rɔ  jóli bɛ́  à jùkɔrɔla láń'í y'á mɛ́ kó : jɔ̀nnin kùnnandi, à fɔ́ "sábabu ɲúman"díɲɛ kùnnangoya fɔ́lɔ yé  mùsojugu fúru yémùso cɛ̀ sàlen bɛ́ kùnnasagon ní syɛ̀ yéà y'á kùnnasiri  à ká ɲùmandɔnbaliya kó lákógo kùnnataní  mùsonin sɔ̀rɔla só, à b'á bá kùnnawolontɛ̀nɛ nàta kùnɲɔgɔnmàa kunntanntɛ̀nɛ nàta kùnɲɔgɔnmàa kùnpa bɔ́né kùnpalen tóra tènmàa kùnpa bɔ́né kùnpalen tóra tènà sàra  bàna kùntaala súrun fɛ̀ntòri yé kúntan yé, nká  Ála b'á fìfamàa kunntankùn tɛ́ cì  kùntigi kɔ́án bɛ́ táa  kùntilenna kélen fɛ̀né má  kùntilenna sɔ̀rɔ  Ncì lá fɔ́len ìn náán ká kán  kà ɲɔ́gɔn kùntilenna dɔ́nné táara  né kùntilenna fɛ̀bálima dɔ́ bólo mána dɛ́sɛ, dɔ́ b'á kùntugusyɔ̀ kútùru = à fàramaàle màsakɛ kùnturu...syɔ̀ kútùru = à fàramaàle màsakɛ kùnturu...jí kɛ́, ń kà  dɔ́ɔnin kùnu

tìle ó tìleSàamori tìle lá...né tìlemana Bàmakɔmɔ̀gɔ tùn bɛ́ tìleminɛnan jɔ̀ màsakɛ kùnnané bɛ́ nà  í tílen fɛ̀ sínià tílennen dòn  tɔ́nsira fɛ̀ kóɲumanà tìlenna  sɛ̀nɛkɛ láà yé  án tìlerɔ ní  sàga kélen yémɔ̀go bɛ́  láyidu tà, Ála dè b'ó tíimɛà ká jàgo tíimɛnaà b'á tími  à ká báara fɛ̀ (kàn)fɔ́ nɛ́nɛ ká tími í lá, í bɛ́ sɛ̀gɛnà b'á tími  à ká báara fɛ̀ (kàn)fɔ́ nɛ́nɛ ká tími í lá, í bɛ́ sɛ̀gɛnní mîn tímina ka dí, à na dòn dá lání mîn tímina ka dí, à na dòn dá lá...kɛ́ ní tíminandiya yéà bɛ́ tìn kànfà yàfara  dén má, kàtugu  à jòli dòn, à tìn b'á látìn tó  ɲɔ́gɔn náà tùn bɛ́ só

Alé sèginbagatɔ, à ká bàbi` kéreweraí tɔ̀ !à tɔ̀ bɔ́ra ń kɔ́nɔdón tɔ̀syɔ̀dun bɛ́ màa kɔ́nɔ tɔ̀nń y'á tà  ń yɛ̀rɛ tɔ̀n nátóbili kɛ́bɛ́ɛ ń'í tòfangasènɲa kélen tɛ́  tógo ncɔ́nìn jíri tɔ́gɔ kó dì ?ù y'á dén tɔ́gɔ dá kó...à bɛ́  í tɔ́gɔ tíɲɛ  í kɔ́
ù tɔ́gɔ bɔ́raà yé  tɔ̀gɔ dòn  dùlɔki láń'í y'á yé fànga dɔ́ɔnin bɛ́ bálikukalan ná, ò bɔ́ra tógodalamɔgɔ lábálikukalan tɔ́gɔladon kɛ́rɛnkɛrɛnnenà tɛ́  táama sà  à màtáama  à kɔ́ kàn
sènnataamaà yé  tìle dúuru ɲɔ̀gɔn táamaù bɛ́  ù bɛ́nba ká làada táamajítolidà dònna  tòli lásù tòlila, à kása bɔ́raNé yé à kɛ́ sù tòlisuma kà cì á nún ná
à tòlisuma tùn bɛ́ kà fɔ́ɔnɔ bìla kɛ̀lɛbolo bɛ́ɛ lájɛlen nácɛ̀nin tólitoli nàtɔ fílɛ !dén màdiya b'á tɔ̀lɔ, nká à t'á mɛ́ɛn sì látómi bìla  í ká kúma ɲɛ́tómi fìlasí bìnna à tɔ̀mɔminɛn kɔ́nɔsí bìnna à tɔ̀mɔminɛn kɔ́nɔkàba` ye tón tàtón bɛ́  bɔ̀lɔ lá, bɔ̀lɔ bɛ́  fɛ́n ná
à yé  tón bìla  à kɛ̀rɛ láà táara í sìgi ò ntòn kùncɛ rɔ́dònso bɛ́  jí tà  k'à bɔ̀n ntòn ná wáasa kà sògo sɔ̀rɔjàkuma y'á tòn  ɲínɛ kànkàbini  ù jɛ̀ra  kà tɔ́n sìgi...í yé  tɔ́n tíɲɛsyɔ̀dun bɛ́ màa kɔ́nɔ tɔ̀nń y'á tà  ń yɛ̀rɛ tɔ̀n nákà jí bìla tɔ̀n ná / sùman sí tɛ́ dénmisɛnnin fɛ̀ tɔ̀n ná bílennìn tɛ́  múra yé bìlen, à kɛ́ra  tónkan yédíɲɛ tónkun náaniù yé  tɔ̀nɔ kɛ́  kà mìsi sànà yé  tɔ̀nɔ sɔ̀rɔ  à láń tɔ̀nɔna  jàgo lásò ní màaninfin kɛ́ra tɔ̀ɲɔgɔnma yéNí í yé í mɔ̀gɔɲɔgɔn dɔ́ ká dùlɔkiba mínɛ tɔ̀nɔmada yé...é 22, 25)à y'à bólo tɔ̀rɔmɔjɔnya shɔ́ láà yé  tɔ̀nɔ sɔ̀rɔ  à láń tɔ̀nɔna  jàgo lásíra mɔ́ɲɔkɔbàna yé  nìn dén mɔ́ɲɔkɔ :nɔ́nfɔn b'í tɔ́nɔtɔnɔ  jíribolo lá  kà yɛ̀lɛnsèntontonmùso ká kán k'í tɔ́n-tɔ́n  kà dén dɛ̀mɛnùmukɛ bɛ́ táa  ɲɔ̀masa tóoma ní  dàba yétɔ́ɔrɔ tɛ́ !
wáasa  í ká sɛ̀gɛn ń'í ká tɔ́ɔrɔ kàna kɛ́  fú yé...kàmiden tɔ́rɔla bìtìga fàrama bɛ́ tɔ́rɔ kà wɔ́rɔà y'á tà  kà tɔ́rɔ  dùgu màgàtigicɛ, ɔ́ tɔ̀rɔmɔjɔn sàba, gátigimuso, tɔ̀rɔmɔjɔn náani, kà Ngála tára ò kànà y'à bólo tɔ̀rɔmɔjɔnya shɔ́ lágàtigicɛ, ɔ́ tɔ̀rɔmɔjɔn sàba, gátigimuso, tɔ̀rɔmɔjɔn náani, kà Ngála tára ò kàngàtigicɛ, ɔ́ tɔ̀rɔmɔjɔn sàba, gátigimuso, tɔ̀rɔmɔjɔn náani, kà Ngála tára ò kànà y'à bólo tɔ̀rɔmɔjɔnya shɔ́ láà y'à bólo tɔ̀rɔmɔjɔnya shɔ́ lágàtigicɛ, ɔ́ tɔ̀rɔmɔjɔn sàba, gátigimuso, tɔ̀rɔmɔjɔn náani, kà Ngála tára ò kàntɔ̀rɔmɔɲɔkokà kɔ́ngɔtɔ  àni  tòtɔ dànbɔ k'ú sí kàna sé  sí mà, ò ká gɛ̀lɛnà y'í tɔ̀tɔma à kɔ́ lámɔ̀gɔ fɔ́lɔ mín yé  tú tìgɛ...ń sèn tùra gùngurun ìn námìsi y'à tùkà tùfa gòsiÁ yé bábili ìn tùfaden fɔ́lɔ dá...à b'á túgu kà kàsi
màa b'í túgu kà ŋúna, à t'í túgu kà wɔ̀silánpa tùguù bɛ́ tùgu  ɲɔ́gɔn nádénnin nàna ni dúmuni yé túgunià ma nà túgundénnin nàna ni dúmuni yé túgunià ma nà túgundénnin nàna ni dúmuni yé túgunià ma nà túgunà túlo bɛ́  nìn bɛ́ɛ rɔ́

hń y'á wéle. Yáa ! à tùn m'á mɛ́nYála  á má  dénnin dɔ́ tɛ̀mɛtɔ yé wá ?ń nàlen à lájɛ  yála né bɛ́  báara sɔ̀rɔ  í fɛ̀yàfa ɲíni màa fɛ̀yàfa ń mà !í kà  ò yàfa  án yé !à yàfara  ù mà mínkɛ...à yé  jàmani fìla yáala
à yé  sò fóni  kà sò yáalagɔ̀fɛ yé  à yàalan ɲúman yéán bɔ́ ó bɔ́ yáalasen fɛ̀, án ká kán k'án tɛ́gɛ kò...í tɛ́gɛ yálon màa túlo kɔ́rɔí jíja yálasa à ka dɔ́ sɔ̀rɔ

í ka à lá dòni tà yála án na wàYála  á má  dénnin dɔ́ tɛ̀mɛtɔ yé wá ?ń nàlen à lájɛ  yála né bɛ́  báara sɔ̀rɔ  í fɛ̀Yála  á má  dénnin dɔ́ tɛ̀mɛtɔ yé wá ?ń nàlen à lájɛ  yála né bɛ́  báara sɔ̀rɔ  í fɛ̀í jíja yálasa à ka dɔ́ sɔ̀rɔ

à dí yàn !yàn ní  tìle sàba cɛ́yànfan fɛ̀kɔ̀nɔ b'á kàma yánkan
nùmumuso bɛ́  fìni yánkan  ù lá  sènɲa sàba, à náaninan, à b'á sìri  ù jù lákɔ̀nɔ b'á kàma yánkan
nùmumuso bɛ́  fìni yánkan  ù lá  sènɲa sàba, à náaninan, à b'á sìri  ù jù láyànni  ò dón kà séyànni  ò dón kà sélàturu (dá / gɔ̀si)  màa yéí dá yáyaya bɔ́ ń ná !ù ye  ɲɔ̀ gòsià kó  à yé

Sèndayɔrɔ ségin bɛ́ à yɛ̀lɛnyɛlɛnnan náí ní  sɛ́nɛ !sɛ̀nɛ kɛ́ò làada ìn bɛ́ sɛ̀nɛ fánaÁn nà dùgukolo sɛ̀nɛbali tó à sàn wólonwulanan náá ká sɛ̀nɛkɛsuman ládonnen kɔ́ (lé 23, 39)ù y'ú sèn fá  kà nàwáasa  í ká sɛ̀gɛn kàna kɛ́  fú yé...sɛ̀gɛn b'á láfàrigan yé  né sɛ̀gɛnsɛ̀nɛ bɛ́  dùgukolo sɛ̀gɛnwáasa  í ká sɛ̀gɛn kàna kɛ́  fú yé...sɛ̀gɛn b'á láfàrigan yé  né sɛ̀gɛnsɛ̀nɛ bɛ́  dùgukolo sɛ̀gɛnà bɛ́ kɔ̀lɔn sènà bɛ́  tìga sènà tɛ́ cì  à sènkala ládúnan sènkɛ́nyɛna ní  dén bángenni yé...háli ní 'póroze' nìn b'án ká làada sɔ̀sɔ, gófɛrɛnaman b'ó sènkɔ̀rɔ̀màdonháli ní 'póroze' nìn b'án ká làada sɔ̀sɔ, gófɛrɛnaman b'ó sènkɔ̀rɔ̀màdonmín sènna ká tɛ́lisènɲa dàma dɔ́  ò kɔ́sènɲa jòlií sénnamɔgɔ yé  í dɔ́gɔnin yé
bìlakoro sénnamɔgɔ yé  bása yémín sènna ká tɛ́li'Á kàna né sènnasiri, kàtugu Ála yé né ká táama díya'

à sí fɔ́ ń yémɔ̀gɔ sí

mùso bɛ́  jɛ́gɛfara syɛ́nsènɲa dàma dɔ́  ò kɔ́sènɲa jòlishìyɛn bɔ́, shìyɛn tàwàa dɔ́ yé  dén yé, wàa dɔ́ yé  nkàmo yé, wàa dɔ́ yé sìyɛn yémùso bɛ jí sɛ́ɛnɛ dúnan kùnkà Masaran ka sɔ̀` kɛ́ tá` lá

kàrisa yé  dùgu sìgi
màsa fìla tɛ́ sìgi  wòlo kélen kànà sìgilen bɛ́ Bàmakɔù ye bìlakorow sìgi  nɛ̀gɛ kɔ́rɔnê tùn ma sìgi ní ò yébáara bɛ́ɛ ká kán kà kɛ́ sìgikafɔ ní dàamu kɔ́nɔ
sìgikafɔ nà kɛ́ Kódiwari kà yɛ̀lɛma dòn jàmana táabolosɛbɛn ná
sìgikafɔ má fɛ́n ó fɛ́n dílan kɛ̀lɛ t'ó dílanní  sìgili kɛ́ra kàban...síganna t'á lá, sán` bɛ́ nà bìMúsà bɛ sìgi-ń-bólo-mà fɛ̀ kósɛbɛMúsà bɛ sìgi-ń-bólo-mà fɛ̀ kósɛbɛní mîn tɛ́ Tàrawele yé, ò yé sìginfɛ yé Fàlajɛní mîn tɛ́ Tàrawele yé, ò yé sìginfɛ yé Fàlajɛsíganna t'á lá, sán` bɛ́ nà bìsìgiɲɔgɔn júgu yé  bàna yé, fúra t'ó láMàli mín yé Kɔ́diwari sìgiɲɔgɔnjamana dɔ́ yé...sìgiɲɔgɔn júgu yé  bàna yé, fúra t'ó láà bɛ́ sígi-sígi  síra láò sàn kélen dúnan mínnu bɛ́ jàgo kɛ́, òlu ká wúsuru sàrata sìgiyɔrɔmana sènɲɛ̀ duuru
sàn 25 ó sàn 25, jàmanaden bɛ́ sìgiyɔrɔma fìlasùgo dára ń náné sùgora  fɛ́n dɔ́ láń bɛ́ síga  à ká kúma náí sìgi í bólo mà !à yé dúmuni sìgi

à sín bɔ́raà sínna  bùgu mà

mùso bɛ́  jɛ́gɛfara syɛ́nsènɲa dàma dɔ́  ò kɔ́sènɲa jòlishìyɛn bɔ́, shìyɛn tàù yé  sìɲɛna kɛ́Sìɲɛnakɛla bɛ́ dùgujɛ màkɔ́nɔí ká nɛ̀gɛso sínga  né màù síngɔ bɛ́  ɲɔ́gɔn ná- jɔ́n yé  síni dɔ́nbaa yé ? - fálatɔ lánaanibaa- jɔ́n yé  síni dɔ́nbaa yé ? - fálatɔ lánaanibaasènɲa dàma dɔ́  ò kɔ́sènɲa jòlisìnɔgɔ b'á ɲɛ́ náí má sùnɔgɔ bán ?fúra y'á sùnɔgɔù bɛ́ táa  ù dá  kà dɔ́ɔnin sùnaaNímafɛn ó fɛ́n ò ní à síɲɔgɔn dè bɛ́ jɛ̀sìsan bɛ́  kɔ̀lɔn ìn kɔ́nɔsìsan b'á láà b'í sínsin  bére lá kà wúlià b'í sínsin  bére lá kà wúlisíra mìn

án bɛ́  síra ɲíni
kà síra dánìn kó tɛ́  í ká síra yéán bɛ́ ò dɔ́n síra jùmɛ fɛ̀ ?síra dànfáralen dòn
díinɛsira táamasìra bánnasíracɛtigɛ ká gɛ̀lɛn sísan, móbili ká cá !síran yé  bɛ́ɛ mìnɛ
síran tɛ́  sàya sàń tɛ́ síran  à ɲɛ́nsìranɛgɛ nùgulen...síratigɛ lá...síratigɛ láí nà kɛ́  màa yé, í tɛ́na sìri  màa násònyalikɛla yé  màa sìri  kà à ká fɛ́n tà...sìrijuru gɛ̀lɛyasìriki sìri  màa kɔ́ fɛ̀fɔ́ sísan
sísan sɔ̀rɔ kà...sìsan bɛ́  kɔ̀lɔn ìn kɔ́nɔsìsan b'á láà bɛ́  sìsi bɔ́à kán sìsilen dònsìsibɔlan mín mànkan mán bòn, ò ntànya bɛ́ ɲàngi dɔ́rɔlɛ 60 nákàrisa sìtanɛ ká bònsùtana dábilakàrisa sìtanɛ ká bònsùtana dábilaù yé jógo mínnu sɔ̀rɔ ù búruju sábabu lá, òlu b'ú bàli kà dòn sìtànɛ̀màko lasènsabana sítununasènsabana sítununaŋɔ́ni yé  né syɛ́n
mùso bɛ́  jɛ́gɛfara syɛ́nsènɲa dàma dɔ́  ò kɔ́sènɲa jòlishìyɛn bɔ́, shìyɛn tàwàa dɔ́ yé  dén yé, wàa dɔ́ yé  nkàmo yé, wàa dɔ́ yé sìyɛn yéń bɛ́ táa  kàrisa ká só
dén sɔ̀rɔla só
só màyɛ́lɛmań bɛ́ táa bɔ́ sósò bòlisìgilan sò ká jàn  dén màkà Masaran ka sɔ̀` kɛ́ tá` lá
jí jìginná à ka shɔ̀ lá, à ka shɔ̀ ɲíginnaà ká sɛ̀bɛnìn yé màa sɛ́bɛ yéù y'á sɛ̀bɛ-fósɛ̀bɛ lá
à b'á sɛ̀bɛ lá
... dòn sɛ̀bɛ láí sɔ̀bɔ ń ná !háli ní í dénmuso fúrula, í ká sóden dònà b'á sɔ̀don  dúmuni nájí kálan fìla tɛ́ sé  kà ɲɔ́gɔn sógindími bɛ mɛ́ í sògo láà yé sògo dúuru fàgaŋɔ́ni yé  à bólo sɔ̀gɔsóda sɔ̀gɔraà y'í bólo sɔ̀gɔ  ɲɔ́gɔn nádùgukolo swàlen dònà yé  ŋɔ́ni sɔ́gɔbɛ kà bɔ́ à sèn náí má né sàgomasɔ̀gɔmà fɛ̀
í ní sɔ̀gɔmà!à yé  ŋɔ́ni sɔ́gɔbɛ kà bɔ́ à sèn náà yé  ŋɔ́ni sɔ́gɔbɛ kà bɔ́ à sèn náfàngalabaara y'á sókarisòku bɛ́ syɛ́nsòli kó fìla tɛ́ sé kà sɔ̀rɔ  sɔ̀gɔmada kélen náù yé  kɔ̀ sòlií dá yé  sòli-kà-bɔ́ kɛ́ dɛ́ !ń bɛ́ ń sòlo dá kàrisa lá
kàrisa sòlo b'í lásɔ́lɔ yé fàn ni ɲɔ́gɔn cɛ́ yésɔ́lɔ yé fàn ni ɲɔ́gɔn cɛ́ yésómɔgɔ dón ?dénmisɛnnin sɔ́mi má sé  báara mín kɛ́li yé, ń'í kó : à k'ò kɛ́, í b'á bànasáni k'à ɲɛ́gan, í k'á sɔ̀mi !dénmisɛnnin sɔ́mi má sé  báara mín kɛ́li yé, ń'í kó : à k'ò kɛ́, í b'á bànacɛ̀ bɛ sɔ̀mi kɛ́ mùso lácɛ̀ bɛ mùso sɔ̀misáni k'à ɲɛ́gan, í k'á sɔ̀mi !ní bángebaa mín sɔ̀mi ká jàn, ò b'á dén dɔ́n kà bɔ́ ɲɔ́gɔn ná
ò kɛ́len mínkɛ, mɔ̀gɔ dɔ́ sɔ̀mi jànyana k'à yé kó :sánì sàmiyɛ kà wósómɔgɔ dón ?á' yé  nsòn bɛ̀n !ntàlen ìn bɛ́ màa sɔ́n hákili (lá)ù bɛ́ sùba sɔ́n ní  syɛ̀ yéà bɛ́  nákɔ sɔ́n wúla fɛ̀díkisɛ bɛ́ wúli ní  ncɔ̀n yéní  Ála sɔ̀nna
à má sɔ̀n  ò màmùso bɛ́ sɔ̀n  à cɛ̀ yéɲɔ̀ má sɔ̀n kósɛbɛ ɲìnadùgu máa tíla, màa sènna bɛ́ sɔ̀nń bɛ́ ń sɔ̀n
ù b'ú sɔ̀n
sán b'á sɔ̀n  nàli lásɔ̀n jàdén bɛ́  mása sɔ̀n tà
sɔ̀n tɛ́  màa mín ná, í júgu b'ó dá  í lá
í sɔ̀n yɛ̀lɛma
à sɔ̀nkɔrɔ dònsɔ̀n kɛ́ra...sɔ̀n ní sɔ̀njùrɔnkolonkàrisa sɔ́nbolo lábilalenné má  mɔ̀gɔ sí sònya ábadajàba sɔ̀ngɔ bìraà bìnnen jí` rɔ́, à sónina  sìyɛn sàbaà bɛ́ kɔ̀lɔn sènà bɛ́  tìga sènà bɛ́  kó bɛ́ɛ bìla  à sɔ̀ni kɔ́rɔntúra bɛ́ jàte sɔ̀ninma fɛ̀à bɛ́  kó bɛ́ɛ bìla  à sɔ̀ni kɔ́rɔà dén tɛ́  sɔ̀njuguya tó yèn, fɔ́ kà táa sàà yé  nìn dúmuni sɔ̀njuguya  à bá kɔ́
í yé  nìn wári sɔ̀njuguya  k'à sɔ̀rɔ  à má d'í màí yé ń sɔ̀njuru tìgɛdùgumɛnɛ sɔ̀nkɔrɔ yé  cínni yé : (pró)ù b'ú sɔ̀nnasiran ní ò kúma cáman yé sáà tó án sɔ̀nnɛmɛ násɔ̀nntan tóra ɲɛ́gɛn nɔ́ò bɛ́ nê mà í ko ntòri jɔ̀len n'à sònsorolenò bɛ́ nê mà í ko ntòri jɔ̀len n'à sònsorolenà bɛ gájiri sɔ́nsɔn dùgu lá
Fàlajɛ dùgu sɔ́nsɔnnen dòn
à ye bìlali sɔ́nsɔnò bɛ́ nê mà í ko ntòri jɔ̀len n'à sònsorolenò bɛ́ nê mà í ko ntòri jɔ̀len n'à sònsorolenò bɛ́ nê mà í ko ntòri jɔ̀len n'à sònsorolenà bìnnen jí` rɔ́, à sónina  sìyɛn sàbané má  mɔ̀gɔ sí sònya ábadané má  mɔ̀gɔ sí sònya ábadaà ye dénmisɛnnin sòonadon à mása yék'án sɔ́ɔni !k'án sɔ́ɔni !nùmukɛ yé  jélekisɛ syɔ́ri  à kàla láà sɔ̀rɔ mán díkà sɔ̀rɔ kɛ́  í yé !í y'á sɔ̀rɔ  sábabu mín ná, í kàn'ó fɔ́  màa sí yé !à yé  wáriba sɔ̀rɔ  jàgo láà y'á sɔ̀rɔ sóà ye dénmisɛnnin sòonadon à mása yéà ye dénmisɛnnin sòonadon à mása yéà ye dénmisɛnnin sòonadon à mása yésósi dá bɛ́ kàrisa láà bɛ gájiri sɔ́nsɔn dùgu lá

à ye bìlali sɔ́nsɔnà bɛ gájiri sɔ́nsɔn dùgu lá

à ye bìlali sɔ́nsɔnsú kòra

sù sɔ́nsùbahanadensúfalendensùgo dára ń náné sùgora  fɛ́n dɔ́ lásùgo dára ń náné sùgora  fɛ́n dɔ́ lásúgu jɔ̀súgunɛ kɛ́súgunɛ kɛ́bàna mín fɔ́li màloya b'í lá, í b'á fɔ́ : sùgurɛ bɛ́ ń násìlamɛ bɛ́ sùjuru bìnsìlamɛ bɛ́ sùjuru bìnà tùn súlenba dònnìn sàmasen sùlilen bɛ́  bíli kɔ́rɔsúma bɔ́
í súma bɔ́'ń bɛ́ kójugu
súma tìgɛ
súma mɛ́njí súma ká díà ká súma kójuguù sìgilen jíri súma nɔ́sú mána kò, dùgukolo bɛ́ súmasánji nàna  fɔ́ kà  dùgukolo sɛ̀bɛ-súmasú mána kò, dùgu bɛ́ súma
kàrisa súmalen
dénmuso kɔ̀ni, Ála y'á dá  à bá yé  k'à dùsu súma, k'à bólo súmaí kà  màlo súmaà yé  Ámadu súma ní  Sáamori yéà yé  kɔ̀nɔ súma ní  màrifa yéjí súma ká díà ká súma kójugusùma ládonsùma ládonní  súmaya má dá kósɛbɛ, kùlu tɛ́ sé kà sɛ̀nɛtò súmayarasánji kó yé ń súmaya  dànni fɛ̀
ò làada bɛ́ kà súmayaà bɛ́  sún ná
sún tìgɛ
sún dòn ( kɛ́ )
dòn  sún náà sunnaà ye tìlè tan sunà y'í súnsìnɔgɔ b'á ɲɛ́ náí má sùnɔgɔ bán ?fúra y'á sùnɔgɔù bɛ́ táa  ù dá  kà dɔ́ɔnin sùnaasùnɔgɔbagatɔ kúnu ká dí  túgubaganci yéà ká súngurun dònà ká súngurun dònà má kɛ́  cɛ̀ fɛ̀, à bɛ́, à súngurunninsìnɔgɔ b'á ɲɛ́ náí má sùnɔgɔ bán ?fúra y'á sùnɔgɔù bɛ́ táa  ù dá  kà dɔ́ɔnin sùnaasùnɔgɔbagatɔ kúnu ká dí  túgubaganci yésúrɔfana mɔ̀naà yé fárakolo cì kúngokolon kɔ́nɔ kà jí súran (kà bɔ́)dúnan dàntigɛbali yé súre yésúrɔfana mɔ̀naà yé  dìngɛn súruku ní  bére yéà yé sà súruku dìngɛn nɔ́à yé  dìngɛn súruku ní  bére yéà yé sà súruku dìngɛn nɔ́né yé  bàba súrukutaama fɔ́ Fàlajɛà ká sùrun Ségu láà ye dénmisɛnnin sòonadon à mása yéà ye dénmisɛnnin sòonadon à mása yéń'í yé né súrundu  nìn kɔ́...
á má ɲɔ́gɔn súuruù yé  jùru sùruntu  sònyalikɛla bólo láń'í yé né súrundu  nìn kɔ́...
á má ɲɔ́gɔn súuruù yé  jùru sùruntu  sònyalikɛla bólo láfìnita sùrunyanadá súsukàrisa sìtanɛ ká bònsùtana dábilaù yé sù sùtarasùtara lání sùtara kɛ́ra, ù bɛ́  ɲɔ́gɔn yécɛ̀ ní  mùso kɛ̀lɛla, mùso súutɛraù yé sù sùtarasùtara lání sùtara kɛ́ra, ù bɛ́  ɲɔ́gɔn yéà fúrakɛtɔ, bànabaatɔ bɛ́ súu fɔ́nìn sàmasen sùlilen bɛ́  bíli kɔ́rɔsúgunɛ kɛ́súgunɛ kɛ́ń'í yé né súrundu  nìn kɔ́...
á má ɲɔ́gɔn súurucɛ̀ ní  mùso kɛ̀lɛla, mùso súutɛracɛ̀ ní  mùso kɛ̀lɛla, mùso súutɛraŋɔ́ni yé  à bólo sɔ̀gɔsóda sɔ̀gɔraà y'í bólo sɔ̀gɔ  ɲɔ́gɔn nádùgukolo swàlen dònŋɔ́ni yé  né syɛ́n
mùso bɛ́  jɛ́gɛfara syɛ́nù bɛ́ɛ lájɛlen yé syɛ̀kasidono yé ù ká tɔ́n ná fàrajɛjamana náí sèn tɛ́  syɛ̀kilifara cìŋɔ́ni yé  né syɛ́n
mùso bɛ́  jɛ́gɛfara syɛ́nsènɲa dàma dɔ́  ò kɔ́sènɲa jòlishìyɛn bɔ́, shìyɛn tàwàa dɔ́ yé  dén yé, wàa dɔ́ yé  nkàmo yé, wàa dɔ́ yé sìyɛn yémùso bɛ jí sɛ́ɛnɛ dúnan kùní jɔ̀ ! án kà  séere ɲíni !né má bɔ́  ò séere màkà Masaran ka sɔ̀` kɛ́ tá` lá
jí jìginná à ka shɔ̀ lá, à ka shɔ̀ ɲíginnanùmukɛ yé  jélekisɛ syɔ́ri  à kàla láà séra sómùn y'í sé  yànni nɔ́ ?fàna má sé bánà séra  mùsofuru yé
à dá séra  à màà séra  à lá
à séra  à kɔ́rɔ
ù bɛ́ sé  bámanakan ná
án tɛ́ sé  kà...
ù séra  ù yɛ̀rɛ láf
